name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guestroom - Atrium-View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:12 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:A very satisfying desert trip. This resort is divided into four islands and three hotels. Yilisha Hotel is outside the scenic area, and Lotus Hotel and Fusha Hotel are inside. The latter two are all-inclusive. Liansha Island and Fusha Island are for accommodation, which are the locations of the two hotels mentioned above, and Xiansha Island and Yuesha Island are for entertainment. There is free transportation between each island, cable car, off-road car, small train or desert yacht, and these transportation tools are very attractive in themselves. Xiansha Island can ride camels, watch performances, and there are various large-scale entertainment facilities similar to amusement parks. There are relatively more people here. Yuesha Island is mainly water activities, and only one of them requires a swimsuit. Camels can also be ridden and performances here, and there are relatively fewer people. Staying at the Lotus Hotel, there is a VIP channel when taking all transportation tools and playing in Xiansha Island, and there is almost no need to wait. Yuesha Island does not have a VIP channel, but there were few people when we went there on the morning of May 4. The service at the Lotus Hotel is very good, and the three meals are also very rich and delicious. There is also a place for children to play in the hotel, a bar where you can drink, and snacks that are served for a long enough time. There was a bonfire party and fireworks show at night, which was very beautiful. I didn't have enough fun, but I highly recommend it.

name:L‚Äça‚Äçd‚Äçy‚Äç ‚ÄçC‚Äça‚Äçt‚ÄçÔøΩ‚ÄçÔøΩ
info:Guestroom - Atrium-View (2 beds)

posted:Posted October 8, 2023
msg:Xiangsha Island has opened three islands: Liansha Island, Xiansha Island, and Yuesha Island
1. The Lotus Hotel is on Liansha Island. Drive to the parking lot of the Lotus Hotel, pack your luggage and take it to the hotel service center. After checking in, a dedicated staff member will check your luggage to the guest room. The process will take about an hour. At this time, the staff will give each guest a bracelet, which is a pass for the whole trip.
2. Take the No. 3 ropeway from the visitor center. There is a special channel for hotel visitors to avoid queuing. The ropeway will reach the midpoint station. Get off the ropeway and take a green jeep to the Lotus Hotel. There will be staff to guide and explain the entire process. After arriving at the hotel, you can go to the room to wash up. We arrived at noon. Have a buffet lunch in the restaurant, a combination of Chinese and Western, including red wine and beer. The variety is very rich! At this time, you can reserve the hot pot buffet for dinner at the front desk and reserve it until 7:30. If you don‚Äôt want to eat hot pot, you can continue with the lunch buffet. After lunch, we took a bus to the midpoint station with signs outside the hotel. If we went to Xiansha Bay, we would take a boat-shaped car, and if we went to Yuesha Bay, we would take a small train. There will be staff to guide you, so you don‚Äôt have to worry about getting lost. Moreover, there are no dedicated channels for bracelet guests to travel the entire journey, so there is no need to queue.
3. There are more entertainment projects in Xiansha Bay, which are relatively exciting. Bracelet guests have special channels without queuing, and there is no limit to the number of times they can play. Fully reflects the superiority! Personally, I prefer the two roller coasters. I basically played the whole process and it took almost three hours. Come out of Xianshawan and return to the starting point, take the transfer bus back to the transfer station, and then take the small train to Yuesha Bay.
4. There are quite a few water sports in Yuesha Bay, including rapids and rafting water slides, but you don‚Äôt need to wear a swimsuit. There is no VIP access here, but there are not many people queuing up, and it gets dark after playing. Just in time to go back to the hotel for dinner.
5. The quality of the hotel's small hot pot buffet is also very high. The beef and dishes are very fresh. There are many staff who actively add soup and alcohol throughout the meal. It is very satisfying. There is a resident bar singer outside in the evening, and there is a bonfire party after eight o'clock. And the drinks in the lobby bar are unlimited. Although the hotel room is not very big, it is very comfortable and clean, and the bath water is very hot and flush. There is no need to worry about the lack of water in the desert.
 6. Pack your luggage and give it to the staff in advance before having buffet breakfast at the hotel the next morning. They will check it in to the customer service center in the parking lot. This process will take an hour. Then have a solid breakfast buffet, the variety is still very rich! After eating and checking out, take a special car to the No. 3 cableway. The staff will cut off the wristband and the cableway will go directly to the parking lot. You can pick up your luggage and get on the car. Don't worry about no one taking care of you during the whole process. The hotel will be responsible to the end. You really can't fault anything! All I can say is that the all-inclusive package is worth every penny!
The above are some of my tips for traveling during the National Day holiday to share with travelers who are planning to stay at the Lotus Hotel. I hope they can help you.

msg:Arrived at the hotel at around 10 am. Booked a family room. The room only includes the price of 2 adults and 1 child. The front desk added money. 1100 for 2 days for a child aged 2-5 years old.
Checked in outside.
There will be a special car to help deliver the luggage to the room.
People need to take the cable car üö° down. Guests staying in the hotel have a special channel. After the cable car comes down, there will be a car to take you to the hotel lobby. There will be a front desk reception. Each person will be given a map of Xiangsha Bay and the time of activities. Explain some hotel room locations and activity locations.

Put down the luggage. Start playing directly.
üé†The main play area is
Yuesha Island. It is mainly water projects. Except for a water park. It is still a bit cold and you can't go into the water. Others basically don't need a swimsuit. Sit in a boat or rubber raft.
Xiansha Island. There are more suitable for adults. Many people under 1.4 meters can't play. You can use the express channel to play on this island with a wristband without queuing.
But bring a baby. There is sand everywhere. Take a shovel and dig wherever you go. It's enough to have fun for a whole day. There are also special areas for children to dig sand on both islands. There are roofs. They won't be exposed to the sun.

The hotel also has many activities during the day and night. But we play outside during the day. I only watched the night activities. Interactive performances. Bonfire parties. Fireworks üéÜ. Stargazing. As long as the weather is good, it will not be cancelled because of few guests.

There are children's sand digging play areas in the hotel. There are outdoor swimming pools and indoor swimming pools. At the current temperature, it's still difficult to go into the water outdoors. In fact, when you come here, the hotel has prepared many things. There are many tools for children in the sand digging area. Raincoats and umbrellas will be prepared when it rains. There are 3 free water bars. It's still very convenient.

The accommodation is definitely not comparable to that in the city. But it's clean. It's still okay. Try not to book an interior view room. It's too small. The overall service is very good. No matter where you go, there will be a car to pick you up. There are many waiters. It feels like they will be by your side at any time. But you have to go to 2 islands to play. One needs to take a train. The other needs to take a desert ship. Although there is no queue in the off-season, it is a waste of time because no one needs to wait for others.

üç¥The hotel includes three meals. All are buffets. Dinner is mainly small hot pot. Compared with the outside, the variety of food is not much. But there are some Mongolian characteristics.
On the first day of check-in, I asked whether lunch would be eaten on the same day or the next day. At that time, I was not informed that lunch would not be served until 12 o'clock. At that time, I thought about going out to play first. So on the last day, I wasted a lunch because I had to catch the train.
In fact, this lunch is a bit tasteless. If you go out to play and come back for lunch, it is very tiring to take a car back and forth. It will take a long time. In fact, the hotel should be more humane. You can choose to include 2 or 3 meals.
There are snack streets on both islands. Xiansha Island is recommended. There are many stalls and many choices.

Many people asked if it would be hot. It would not be stuffy. As long as there is a cool place, it would be fine. There are also wooden planks in the desert. There are parasols all over the road‚õ±Ô∏èOne day it rained at night. It was still a bit cool to go out during the day. So you need to prepare long sleeves.

‚ùóÔ∏èThere is a travel photo shoot in the hotel. My friend came before. The lowest price was 199. Now the price has increased to the lowest price of 588üòÇ. Clothes need to be charged separately. There is a water bar near the ** in Yuesha Island. You can rent Mongolian clothes for 20üí∞. You can change your clothes and take photos at will. The uncle is also very nice. Whether you consume or not, he will be very enthusiastic. He will answer all questions.
You can bring a sandboard yourself. It seems to be 80. Sandboarding alone is not included. 20 per time.

‚ùóÔ∏èYou will also take pictures of each play project. If you need to plasticize the photo 15, it will be 20. It also captures everyone's rare visit to the desertüèúÔ∏è. It's not a small amount of moneyüòÇ

In fact, this hotel is enough for one night. At that time, I was worried that the second child would not be able to hold on at noon. But he loves to dig sand. He holds a shovel in his hand. Basically, he digs wherever he goes. He doesn't sleep. The two islands are closed at 6 o'clock, and dinner is from 6:30 to 9 o'clock. You can rest after you come back. Check out the next day.
